 <div n="19" type="adhyāya">
  <head>ekonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.1"><label>ci.19.1</label> athāto vṛddhyupadaṃśaślīpadacikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.2"><label>ci.19.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.3"><label>ci.19.3</label> antravṛddhyā vinā ṣaḍyā vṛddhayas tāsu varjayet |
  aśvādiyānaṃ vyāyāmaṃ maithunaṃ veganigraham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.4"><label>ci.19.4</label> atyāsanaṃ caṅkramaṇam upavāsaṃ gurūṇi ca |
  tatrādito vātavṛddhau traivṛtasnigdhamāturam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.5"><label>ci.19.5</label> svinnaṃ cainaṃ yathānyāyaṃ pāyayeta virecanam |
  kośāmratilvakair aṇḍaphalatailāni vā naram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.6"><label>ci.19.6</label> sakṣīraṃ vā pibenmāsaṃ tailameraṇḍasaṃbhavam |
  tataḥ kāle 'nilaghnānāṃ kvāthaiḥ kalkaiś ca buddhimān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.7"><label>ci.19.7</label> nirūhayen nirūḍhaṃ ca bhuktavantaṃ rasaudanam |
  yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tatas tailena yojayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.8"><label>ci.19.8</label> snehopanāhau kuryāc ca pradehāṃś cānilāpahān |
  vidagdhāṃ pācayitvā vā sevanīṃ parivarjayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.9"><label>ci.19.9</label> bhindyāttataḥ prabhinnāyāṃ yathoktaṃ kramam ācaret
  | pittajāyāmapakvāyāṃ pittagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.10"><label>ci.19.10</label> pakvāṃ vā bhedayed bhinnāṃ śodhayet
  kṣaudrasarpiṣā | śuddhāyāṃ ca bhiṣagdadyāttailaṃ kalkaṃ ca ropaṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.11"><label>ci.19.11</label> raktajāyāṃ jalaukobhiḥ <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śoṇitaṃ nirharedbhiṣak | pibed virecanaṃ vā 'pi
  śarkarākṣaudrasaṃyutam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.12"><label>ci.19.12</label> pittagranthikramaṃ kuryād āme pakve ca sarvadā |
  vṛddhiṃ kaphātmikāmuṣṇair mūtrapiṣṭaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.13"><label>ci.19.13</label> pītadārukaṣāyaṃ ca piben mūtreṇa saṃyutam |
  vimlāpanād ṛte vā 'pi śleṣmagranthikramo hitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.14"><label>ci.19.14</label> pakvāyāṃ ca vibhinnāyāṃ tailaṃ śodhanamiṣyate |
  sumanāruṣkarāṅkoṭhasaptaparṇeṣu sādhitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.15"><label>ci.19.15</label> medaḥsamutthāṃ saṃsvedya lepayet surasādinā |
  śirovirekadravyair vā sukhoṣṇair mūtrasaṃyutaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.16"><label>ci.19.16</label> svinnāṃ cāveṣṭya paṭṭena samāśvāsya tu mānavam |
  rakṣan phale sevanīṃ ca vṛddhipatreṇa dārayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.17"><label>ci.19.17</label> medas tataḥ samuddhṛtya dadyāt kāsīsasaindhave |
  badhnīyāc ca yathoddiṣṭaṃ śuddhe tailaṃ ca dāpayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.18"><label>ci.19.18</label> manaḥśilālalavaṇaiḥ siddhamāruṣkareṣu ca |
  mūtrajāṃ svedayitvā tu vastrapaṭṭena veṣṭayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.19"><label>ci.19.19</label> sevanyāḥ pārśvato 'dhastād vidhyed vrīhimukhena
  tu | athātra dvimukhāṃ nāḍīṃ dattvā visrāvayed bhiṣak || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.20"><label>ci.19.20</label> mūtraṃ nāḍīm athoddhṛtya sthagikābandham ācaret
  | śuddhāyāṃ ropaṇaṃ dadyād varjayed antrahaitukīm || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.21"><label>ci.19.21</label> aprāptaphalakoṣāyāṃ vātavṛddhikramo hitaḥ |
  tatra yā vaṅkhaṇasthā <ref rend="superscript footnote
  marker">*</ref>tāṃ dahedardhenduvattrayā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.22"><label>ci.19.22</label> samyaṅmārgāvarodhārthaṃ kośaprāptāṃ tu varjayet
  | tvacaṃ bhittvā 'ṅguṣṭhamadhye dahec cāṅgaviparyayāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.23"><label>ci.19.23</label> anenaiva vidhānena vṛddhī vātakaphātmike |
  pradahet prayataḥ kiṃtu snāyucchedo 'dhikastayoḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.24"><label>ci.19.24</label> śaṅkhopari ca karṇānte tyaktvā yatnena sevanīm |
  vyatyāsādvā sirāṃ vidhyedantravṛddhinivṛttaye || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.25"><label>ci.19.25</label> upadaṃśeṣu sādhyeṣu snigdhasvinnasya dehinaḥ |
  sirāṃ vidhyenmeḍhramadhye pātayed vā jalaukasaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.26"><label>ci.19.26</label> hared ubhayataś cāpi doṣān atyartham ucchritān |
  sadyo 'pahṛtadoṣasya rukśophāv upaśāmyataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.27"><label>ci.19.27</label> yadi vā durbalo jantur na vā prāptaṃ virecanam |
  nirūheṇa haret tasya doṣān atyartham ucchritān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.28"><label>ci.19.28</label> prapauṇḍarīkayaṣṭyāhvavarṣābhūkuṣṭhadārubhiḥ |
  saralāgururāsnābhir vātajaṃ saṃpralepayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.29"><label>ci.19.29</label> niculair aṇḍabījāni yavagodhūmasaktavaḥ | etaiś
  ca vātajaṃ snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ saṃpralepayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.30"><label>ci.19.30</label> prapauṇḍarīkapūrvaiś ca dravyaiḥ sekaḥ
  praśasyate | gaurikāñjanayaṣṭyāhvārivośīrapadmakaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.31"><label>ci.19.31</label> sacandanotpalaiḥ snigdhaiḥ paittikaṃ
  saṃpralepayet | padmotpalamṛṇālaiś ca sasarjārjunavetasaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.32"><label>ci.19.32</label> sarpiḥsnigdhaiḥ samadhukaiḥ paittikaṃ
  saṃpralepayet | secayec ca ghṛtakṣīraśarkarekṣumadhūdakaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.33"><label>ci.19.33</label> athavā 'pi suśītena kaṣāyeṇa vaṭādinā |
  sālāśvakarṇājakarṇadhavatvagbhiḥ kaphotthitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.34"><label>ci.19.34</label> surāpiṣṭābhir uṣṇābhiḥ satailābhiḥ pralepayet |
  rajanyativiṣāmustāsurāsuradārubhiḥ<ref rend="superscript
  footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.35"><label>ci.19.35</label> saptrapāṭhāpattūrair athavā saṃpralepayet |
  surasāragvadhādyoś ca kvāthābhyāṃ paribecayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.36a"> evaṃ saṃśodhanālepasekaśoṇitamokṣaṇaiḥ | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.36b"> pratikuryāt  kriyāyogaiḥ prāksthānoktair hitair api || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.37a"><label>ci.19.37a</label> na yāti ca yathā pākaṃ prayateta tathā bhiṣak
  | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.37b"><label>ci.19.37b</label>vidagdhais tu sirāsnāyutvaṅmāṃsaiḥ kṣīyate
  dhvajaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.38"><label>ci.19.38</label> śastreṇopacarec cāpi pākamāgatamāśu vai | tadā
  'pohya tilaiḥ sarpiḥkṣaudrayuktaiḥ pralepayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.39"><label>ci.19.39</label> karavīrasya patrāṇi jātyāragvadhayos tathā |
  prakṣālane prayojyāni vaijayantyarkayor api || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.40"><label>ci.19.40</label> saurāṣṭrīṃ gair ikaṃ tutthaṃ
  puṣpakāsīsasaindhavam | rodhraṃ rasāñjanaṃ dārvīṃ haritālaṃ manaḥśilām || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.41"><label>ci.19.41</label> hareṇukaile ca tathā sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet |
  taccūrṇaṃ kṣaudrasaṃyuktam upadaṃśeṣu pūjitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.42"><label>ci.19.42</label> jambvāmrasumanānimbaśvetakāmbojipallavāḥ |
  śallakībadarībilvapalāśatiniśatvacaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.43"><label>ci.19.43</label> kṣīriṇāṃ ca tvaco yojyāḥ kvāthe triphalayā saha
  | tena kvāthena niyataṃ vraṇaṃ prākṣālayed bhiṣak || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.44"><label>ci.19.44</label> asminn eva kaṣāye tu tailaṃ dhīro vipācayet |
  gojīviḍaṅgayaṣṭībhiḥ sarvagandhaiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.45a"><label>ci.19.45a</label> etat sarvopadaṃśeṣu śreṣṭhaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.45b"><label>ci.19.45b</label>svarjikātutthakāsīsaṃ śaileyaṃ ca rasāñjanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.46"><label>ci.19.46</label> manaḥśilāsamaiścūrṇaṃ vraṇavīsśarpanāśanam |
  gundrāṃ dagdhvā kṛtaṃ bhasma haritālaṃ manaḥśilā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.47"><label>ci.19.47</label> upadaṃśabisarpāṇāmetacchantikaraṃ param |
  mārkavastriphalā dantī tāmracūrṇamayor ajaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.48a"><label>ci.19.48a</label> upadaṃśaṃ nihantyeṣa vṛkṣamindrāśaniryathā | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.48b"><label>ci.19.48b</label> upadaṃśadvaye 'pyetāṃ pratyākhyāyācaret kriyām
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.49a"><label>ci.19.49a</label> tayor eva ca yā yogyā vīkṣya doṣabalābalam | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.49b"><label>ci.19.49b</label> upadaṃśe viśeṣeṇa śṛṇu bhūyastridoṣaje || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.50"><label>ci.19.50</label> duṣṭavraṇavidhiṃ kuryāt kuthitaṃ mehanaṃ tyajet
  | jambvoṣṭhenāgnivarṇena paś cāccheṣaṃ dahedbhiṣak || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.51"><label>ci.19.51</label> samyagdagdhaṃ ca vijñāya madhusarpiḥ prayojayet
  | śuddhe ca ropaṇaṃ dadyāt kalkaṃ tailaṃ hitaṃ ca yat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.52"><label>ci.19.52</label> snehasvedopapanne tu ślīpade 'nilane bhiṣak |
  kṛtvā gulphopari sirāṃ vidhyet tu caturaṅgule || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.53"><label>ci.19.53</label> samāpyāyitadehaṃ ca bastibhiḥ samupācaret |
  māsameraṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ piben mūtreṇa saṃyutam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.54"><label>ci.19.54</label> payasaudanamaśnīyānnāgarakvathitena ca |
  taivṛtaṃ copayuñjīta śasto dāhas tathā 'gninā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.55"><label>ci.19.55</label> gulphasyādhaḥ sirāṃ vidhyecchlīpade
  pittasaṃbhave | pītaghnīṃ ca kriyāṃ kuryāt pittārbudavisarpavat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.56"><label>ci.19.56</label> sirāṃ suviditāṃ vidhyedaṅguṣṭhe ślaiṣmike bhiṣak
  | madhuyuktāni cābhīkṣṇaṃ kaṣāyāṇi piben naraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.57"><label>ci.19.57</label> pibedvā 'pyabhayākalkaṃ mūtreṇānyatamena ca |
  kaṭukāmamṛtāṃ śuṇṭhīṃ viḍaṅgaṃ dāru citrakam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.58"><label>ci.19.58</label> hitaṃ vā lepane nityaṃ bhadradāru sacitrakam |
  viḍaṅgamaricārkeṣu nāgare citrake 'thavā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.59"><label>ci.19.59</label> bhadradārvelukākhye ca sarveṣu lavaṇeṣu ca |
  tailaṃ pakvaṃ pibedvā 'pi yavānnaṃ ca hitaṃ sadā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.60"><label>ci.19.60</label> pibet sarṣapatailaṃ vā ślīpadānāṃ nivṛttaye |
  pūtīkarañjapatrāṇāṃ rasaṃ vā 'pi yathābalam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.61"><label>ci.19.61</label> anenaiva vidhānena putrañjīvakajaṃ rasam |
  prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ kālasātmyavibhāgavit || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.62"><label>ci.19.62</label> kevukākandaniryāsaṃ lavaṇaṃ tvatha pākimam |
  rasaṃ dattvā 'tha pūrvoktaṃ peyametadbhiṣagjitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.63"><label>ci.19.63</label> kākādanīṃ kākajaṅghāṃ bṛhatīṃ kaṇṭakārikām |
  kadambapuṣpīṃ mandārīṃ lambāṃ śukanasāṃ tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.64"><label>ci.19.64</label> dagdhvā mūtreṇa tadbhasma srāvayet kṣārakalpavat
  | tatra dadyāt pratīvāpaṃ kākodumbarikārasam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.65"><label>ci.19.65</label> madanāc ca phalāt kvāthaṃ śukākhyasvarasaṃ tathā
  | eṣa kṣāras tu pānīyaḥ ślīpadaṃ hanti sevitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.66"><label>ci.19.66</label> apacīṃ galagaṇḍaṃ ca grahaṇīdoṣam eva ca |
  bhaktasyānaśanaṃ caiva hanyāt sarvaviṣāṇi ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.67"><label>ci.19.67</label> eṣv eva tailaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ nasyābhyaṅgeṣu pūjitam
  | etān evāmayān hanti ye ca duṣṭavraṇā nṛṇām || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.68"><label>ci.19.68</label> dravantīṃ trivṛtāṃ dantīṃ nīlīṃ śyāmāṃ tathaiva
  ca | saptalāṃ śaṅkhinīṃ caiva dagdhvā mūtreṇa gālayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.19.69"><label>ci.19.69</label> dadyāc ca triphalākvātham eṣa kṣāras tu sādhitaḥ
  | adho gacchati pītas tu pūrvaiś cāpyāśiṣaḥ samāḥ ||</l>

  nāmaikonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||19 ||</p>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.36"><label>ci.20.36</label> kṣaudrājyayuktayā limpeddaṃṣṭrayā śūkarasya ca |

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.37-38a"><label>ci.20.37-38a</label> yauvane piḍakāsveṣa viśeṣācchardanaṃ

  lepanaṃ ca vacārodhrasaindhavaiḥ sarṣapānvitaiḥ ||
  <caesura/>
  kustumburuvacālodhrakuṣṭharvā lepanaṃ hitam | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38i"/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38ii"/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.38b-39a"><label>ci.20.38b-39a</label> padminīkaṇṭake roge
  chardayennimbavāriṇā ||
  <caesura/>
  tenaiva siddhaṃ sakṣaudraṃ sarpiḥpānaṃ pradāpayet | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.39b"><label>ci.20.39b</label> nimbāragvadhayoḥ kalko hita utsādane bhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.40-41"><label>ci.20.40-41</label> parivṛttiṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ susvinnām
  upanāhayet |
  <caesura/>
  tato 'bhyajya śanaiś carma cānayet pīḍayenmaṇim ||
  <caesura/>
  praviṣṭe ca maṇau carma svedayed upanāhanaiḥ |
  <caesura/>
  trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā vātaghnaiḥ sālvaṇādibhiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.42"><label>ci.20.42</label> dadyādvātaharān bastīn snigdhānyannāni bhojayet 
  | vapāṭikāṃ jayed evaṃ yathādoṣaṃ cikitsakaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.43"><label>ci.20.43</label> niruddhaprakaśe nāḍīṃ lauhīmubhayatomukhīm |
  dāravīṃ vā jatukṛtāṃ ghṛtābhyaktāṃ praveśayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.44"><label>ci.20.44</label> pariṣeke vasāmajjaśiśumāravarāhayoḥ |
  cakratailaṃ tathā yojyaṃ vātaghnadravyasaṃyutam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.45"><label>ci.20.45</label> tryahāttryahāt sthūlatarāṃ samyaṅnāḍīṃ
  praveśayet | sroto vivardhayed evaṃ snigdhamannaṃ ca bhojayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46a"><label>ci.20.46a</label> bhittvā vā sevanīṃ muktvā sadyaḥkṣatavadācaret
  |</l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.46b-47a"><label>ci.20.46b-47a</label> sanniruddhagudaṃ rogaṃ valmīkaṃ
  vahnirohiṇīm ||
  <caesura/>
  pratyākhyāya yathāyogaṃ cikitsitamathācaret |</l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.47b"><label>ci.20.47b</label> visarpoktena vidhinā sādhayed agnirohiṇīm || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48a"><label>ci.20.48a</label> sanniruddhagude yojyā niruddhaprakaśakriyā | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.48b-49"><label>ci.20.48b-49</label> śastreṇotkṛtya valmīkaṃ kṣārāgnibhyāṃ

  <caesura/>
  vidhānenārbudoktena śodhayitvā ca ropayet |
  <caesura/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.50"><label>ci.20.50</label> tatra saṃśodhanaṃ kṛtvā śoṇitaṃ mokṣayed bhiṣak |
  kulatthikāyā mūlaiś ca guḍūcyā lavaṇena ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.51"><label>ci.20.51</label> ārevatasya mūlaiś ca dantīmūlais tathaiva ca |

  yathākramam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.54"><label>ci.20.54</label> vraṇaṃ viśuddhaṃ vijñāya ropayenmatimān bhiṣak |
  sumanā granthayaś caiva bhallātakamanaḥśile || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.20.55"><label>ci.20.55</label> kālānusārī sūkṣmailā candanāguruṇī tathā | etaiḥ
  siddhaṃ nimbatailaṃ valmīke ropaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

     <head>ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1"><label>ci.21.1</label> athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"><label>ci.21.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3"><label>ci.21.3</label> saṃlikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet |
      <caesura/>
       kaṣāyeṣv eva tailaṃ ca kurvīta vraṇaropaṇam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4"><label>ci.21.4</label> aṣṭhīlikāṃ jalaukobhirgrāhayecca<ref
       rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> punaḥ punaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       tathā cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivad uddharet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5"><label>ci.21.5</label> svedayed grathitaṃ śaśvannāḍīsvedena buddhimān |
      <caesura/>
       sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susnigdhair upanāhayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6"><label>ci.21.6</label> kumbhīkāṃ pākamāpannāṃ bhindyācchuddhāṃ tu ropayet
      |
      <caesura/>
       tailena triphalālodhratindukāmrātakena tu || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7"><label>ci.21.7</label> grāhayitvā jalaukobhir alajīṃ secayet tataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kaṣāyais teṣu siddhaṃ ca tailaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8"><label>ci.21.8</label> balātailena koṣṇena mṛditaṃ pariṣecayet |
      <caesura/>
       bhadhuraiḥ sarpiṣā snigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9"><label>ci.21.9</label> saṃmūḍhapiḍakāṃ kṣipraṃ jalaukobhir upācaret |
      <caesura/>
       bhittvā paryāgatāṃ cāpi lepayet kṣaudrasarpiṣā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10"><label>ci.21.10</label> avamanthe gate pākaṃ bhinne tailaṃ vidhīyate |
      <caesura/>
       dhavāśvakarṇapattaṅgasallakītindukīkṛtam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11"><label>ci.21.11</label> kriyāṃ puṣkarikāyāṃ tu śītāṃ sarvāṃ prayojayet |
      <caesura/>
       jalaukobhirhareccāsṛk sarpiṣā cāvasecayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12"><label>ci.21.12</label> sparśahānyāṃ hared raktaṃ pradihyānmadhurair api
      |
      <caesura/>
       kṣīrekṣurasasarpirbhiḥ secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13"><label>ci.21.13</label> piḍakām uttamākhyāṃ ca baḍiśenoddhared bhiṣak |
      <caesura/>
       uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14"><label>ci.21.14</label> rasakriyā vidhātavyā likhite śataponake |
      <caesura/>
       pṛthak parṇyādisiddhaṃ ca deyaṃ tailam anantaram || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15"><label>ci.21.15</label> kriyāṃ kuryād bhiṣak prājñastvakpākasya
      visarpavat |
      <caesura/>
       raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyā śoṇitaje 'rbude || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16"><label>ci.21.16</label> kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi tailaṃ cūrṇaṃ rasakriyām |
      <caesura/>
       śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17"><label>ci.21.17</label> hitaṃ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ pathyaṃ cāpi cirecanam |
      <caesura/>
       hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18"><label>ci.21.18</label> arbudaṃ māṃsapākaṃ ca vidradhiṃ tilakālakam |
      <caesura/>
       pratyākhyāya prakurvīta bhiṣak samyak pratikriyām ||</l>

     <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne śūkarogacikitsitaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
      ||21 ||</p>

 <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
  <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1"><label>ci.23.1</label> athātaḥ śophānāṃ cikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"><label>ci.23.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3"><label>ci.23.3</label> ṣaḍvidho 'vayavasamutthaḥ
  śopho 'bhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratīkārataś ca; sarvasaras tu pañcavidhaḥ, tadyathā
  vātapittaśleṣmasannipātaviṣanimittaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4"><label>ci.23.4</label>
  tatrāpatarpitasyādhvagamanādatimātramabhyavaharato vā
  piṣṭānnaharitakaśākalavaṇāni kṣīṇasya vā 'timātramamlam upasevamānasya
  mṛtpakvaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarānūpaudakamāṃsasevanādajīrṇino vā
  grāmyadharmasevanādviruddhāhārasevanāt vā
  hastyaśvoṣṭrarathapadātisaṅkṣobhaṇādayo sitasya doṣā dhātūn pradūṣya
  śvayathumāpādayantyakhile śarīre || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5"><label>ci.23.5</label> tatra vātaśvayathuraruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
  mṛduranavasthitāstodādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; pittaśvayathuḥ pītaḥ sarakto
  vā mṛduḥ śīghrānusāryūṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ; śleṣmaśvayathuḥ pāṇḍuḥ
  śuklo vā snigdhaḥ kaṭhinaḥ śīto mandānusārī, kaṇḍvādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣāḥ;
  sannipātaśvayathuḥ sarvavarṇavedanaḥ; viṣanimittastu
  garopayogādduṣṭatoyasevanāt prakuthitodakāvagāhanāt
  saviṣasattvadigdhacūrṇāvacūrṇanādvā saviṣamūtrapurīṣaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā
  tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśanāt, sa tu mṛduḥ ksiprotthāno 'valambī calo 'calo vā
  dāhapākarāgaprāyaś ca bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6"><label>ci.23.6</label> bhavanti cātra doṣāḥ
  śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi kurvantyāmāśayasthitāḥ | pakvāśayasthā madhye ca
  varcaḥsthānagatāstvadhaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7"><label>ci.23.7</label> kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ kuryuḥ
  sarvasaraṃ tathā | śvayathurmadhyadeśe yaḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8"><label>ci.23.8</label> ardhāṅge 'riṣṭabhūtaś ca yaścordhvaṃ
  parisarpati | śvāsaḥ pipāsā daurbalyaṃ jvaraścchardirarocakaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9"><label>ci.23.9</label> hikkātīsārakāsāś ca śūnaṃ
  saṅkṣapayanti hi | sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10"><label>ci.23.10</label> śophinaḥ sarva eva
  parihareyuramlalavaṇadadhiguḍavasāpayastailaghṛtapiṣṭamayagurūṇi || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11"><label>ci.23.11</label> tatra vātaśvayathau
  traivṛtameraṇḍatailaṃ vā māsamardhamāsaṃ vā pāyayet,
  nyagrodhādikakaṣāyasiddhaṃ sarpiḥ pittaśvayathau, āragvadhādisiddhaṃ sarpiḥ
  śleṣmaśvayathau, sannipātaśvayathau snuhīkṣīrapātraṃ dvādaśabhir amlapātraiḥ
  pratisaṃsṛjya dantīdravantīpratīvāpaṃ sarpiḥ pācayitvā pāyayet,
  viṣanimitteṣu kalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12"><label>ci.23.12</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ
  sāmānyacikitsitam upadekṣyāmaḥ tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktānyudareṣu
  tato 'nyatamanupayujyamānaṃ śvayathumapahanti, mūtravartikriyāṃ vā seveta,
  navāyasaṃ vā 'haraharmadhunā,
  viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricacūrṇaṃ vā dharaṇamuṣṇāmbunā,
  trikaṭukṣārāyaścūrṇāni vā triphalākaṣāyeṇa, mūtraṃ vā tulyakṣīraṃ, harītakīṃ
  vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta, devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā, gugguluṃ vā mūtreṇa
  varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā, tulyaguḍaṃ vā mūtreṇa varṣabhūkaṣāyānupānaṃ vā,
  tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ vā, varṣābhūkaṣāyaṃ mūlakalkaṃ vā saśṛṅgaveraṃ
  payo 'nupānamaharaharmāsaṃ, vyoṣavarṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā sarpiṣā
  mudgolumbān bhakṣayet, pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakamayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ
  vā kṣīraṃ pibet, sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddhaṃ vā, trikaṭukair
  aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddhaṃ vā, varṣābhūśṛṅgaverasahādevadārusiddhaṃ vā,
  tathā 'lābubibhītakaphalakalkaṃ vā taṇḍulāmbunā;
  kṣīrapippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpasnehena
  bhojayed yavānnaṃ godhūmānnaṃ vā; vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimbavarṣābhūkvāthaiś ca
  pariṣekaḥ; sarṣapasuvarcalāsaindhavaśārṅgeṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ;
  yathādoṣaṃ ca vamanavirecanāsthāpanāni tīkṣṇānyajasram upaseveta,
  snehasvedopanāhāṃś ca; sirābhiś cābhīkṣṇaṃ
  śoṇitamavasecayed anyatropadravaśophāditi || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13"><label>ci.23.13</label> bhavati cātra piṣṭānnamamlaṃ
  lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamajāṅgalaṃ ca | striyo ghṛtaṃ tailapayogurūṇi
  śophaṃ jighāṃsuḥ parivarjayet tu ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sothacikitsitaṃ nāma
  trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||23 ||</p>
 </div>

  <head>caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.1"><label>ci.24.1</label> athāto 'nāgatābādhāpratiṣedhaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.2"><label>ci.24.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.3"><label>ci.24.3</label> utthāyotthāya satataṃ svasthenārogyamicchatā |
  <caesura/>
  dhīmatā yadanuṣṭheyaṃ tat sarvaṃ saṃpravakṣyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.4"><label>ci.24.4</label> tatrādau <ref rend="superscript
  footnote marker">*</ref>dantapavanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulamāyatam |
  <caesura/>
  kaniṣṭhikāparīṇāhamṛjvagranthitamavraṇam<ref rend="superscript footnote
  marker">*</ref> || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.5"><label>ci.24.5</label> ayugmagranthi yac cāpi pratyagraṃ śastabhūmijam |
  <caesura/>
  avekṣyartuṃ ca doṣaṃ ca rasaṃ vīryaṃ ca yojayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.6"><label>ci.24.6</label> kaṣāyaṃ madhuraṃ tiktaṃ kaṭukaṃ prātarutthitaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  nimbaś ca tiktake śreṣṭhaḥ kaṣāye khadiras tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.7"><label>ci.24.7</label> madhūko madhure śreṣṭhaḥ karañjaḥ kaṭuke tathā |
  <caesura/>
  kṣaudravyoṣatrivargāktaṃ satailaṃ saindhavena ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.8"><label>ci.24.8</label> cūrṇena tejovatyāś ca dantānnityaṃ viśodhayet |
  ekaikaṃ ghrṣayed dantaṃ mṛdunā kūrcakena ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.89"><label>ci.24.89</label> tatrādita eva nīcanakharomṇā śucinā śuklavāsasā
  laghūṣṇīṣacchatropānatkena daṇḍapāṇinā kāle hitamitamadhurapūrvābhibhāṣiṇā bandhubhūtena
  bhūtānāṃ guruvṛddhānumatena susahāyenānanyamanasā khalūpacaritavyaṃ, tadapi na rātrau, na
  keśāsthikaṇṭakāśmatuṣabhasmotkarakapālāṅgārāmedhyasnānabalibhūmiṣu, na
  viṣamendrakīlacatuṣpathaśvabhrāṇām upariṣṭāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.90"><label>ci.24.90</label> na rājadviṣṭaparuṣapaiśunyānṛtāni vadet, na
  devabrāhmaṇapitṛparivādāṃś ca; na narendradviṣṭonmattapatitakṣudranīcānupāsīta || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.91"><label>ci.24.91</label>
  vṛkṣaparvataprapātaviṣamavalmīkaduṣṭavājikuñjarādyadhirohaṇāni pariharet,
  pūrṇanadīsamudrāviditapalvalaśvabhrakūpāvataraṇāni,
  bhinnaśūnyāgāraśmaśānavijanāraṇyavāsāgnisaṃbhramavyālabhujaṅgakīṭasevāś ca,
  grāmāghātakalahaśastrasannipātavyālasarīsṛpaśṛṅgisannikarṣāṃś ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.92"><label>ci.24.92</label> nāgnigogurubrāhmaṇapreṅkhādampatyantareṇa yāyāt
  | na śavamanuyāyāt | devagobrāhmaṇacaityadhvajarogipatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca chāyāṃ nākrameta |
  nāstaṃ gacchantamudyantaṃ vā++ādityaṃ vīkṣeta | gāṃ dhāpayantīṃ dhayantīṃ paraśasyaṃ vā
  carantīṃ na kasmaicidācakṣīta, na colkāpātotpātendradhanūṃṣi | nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamet | nāpo
  bhūmiṃ vā pāṇipādenābhihanyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.93"><label>ci.24.93</label> na vegān dhārayed vātamūtrapurīṣādīnām | na
  bahirvegān grāmanagaradevatāyatanaśmaśānacatuṣpathasalilāśayapathisannikṛṣṭāvutsṛjenna
  prakāśaṃ na vāyvagnisalilasomārkagogurupratimukham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.94"><label>ci.24.94</label> na bhūmiṃ vilikhet, nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ sadasi
  jṛmbhodagārakāsaśvāsakṣavathūnutsṛjet, na paryaṅkikāvaṣṭambhapādaprasāraṇāni gurusannidhau
  kuryāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.95"><label>ci.24.95</label> na
  bālakarṇanāsāsrotodaśanākṣivivarāṇyabhikuṣṇīyāt<ref rend="superscript
  footnote marker">*</ref>, na vījayet keśamukhanakhavastragātrāṇi, na
  gātranakhavaktravāditraṃ kuryāt , na kāṣṭhaloṣṭatṛṇādīnabhihanyācchindyādbhindyādvā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.96"><label>ci.24.96</label> na prativātātapaṃ seveta, na bhuktamātro
  'gnimupāsīta, notkaṭakālpakāṣṭhāsanamadhyāsīta, na grīvāṃ viṣamaṃ dhārayet, na viṣamakāyaḥ
  kriyāṃ bhajeta bhuñjīta vā, na pratatamīkṣeta viśeṣājjyotirbhāskarasūkṣmacalabhrāntāni, na
  bhāraṃ śirasā vahet, na
  svapnajāgaraṇaśayanāsanasthānacaṅkramaṇayānavāhanapradhāvanalaṅghanaplavanaprataraṇahāsyabhāṣyavyavāyavyāyāmādīnucitānapyatiseveta
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.97"><label>ci.24.97</label> ucitādapyahitāt kramaśo viramet,
  hitamanucitamapyaseveta kramaśaḥ, na caikāntataḥ pādahīnāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.98"><label>ci.24.98</label> nāvākśirāḥ śayīta, na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta, na
  vinā pātreṇa, nāñjalipuṭenāpaḥ pibet, kāle hitamitasnigdhamadhuraprāyamāhāraṃ
  vaidyapratyavekṣitamaśnīyāt, grāmagaṇagaṇikāpaṇikaśatrusatraśaṭhapatitabhojanāni parikaret,
  śeṣāṇyapi cāniṣṭarūparasagandhasparśaśabdamānasāni, anyānyevaṃguṇānyapi saṃbhramadattāni,
  (tānyapi) <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>makṣikābālopahatāni, nāprakṣālitapādo
  bhuñjīta na mūtroccārapīḍito na sandhyayor nānupāśrito nātītakālaṃ hīnamatimātraṃ
  (noddhṛtasnehaṃ) ceti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"><label>ci.24.99</label> na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ naṣṭaṃ paryuṣitaṃ payaḥ
  | na naktaṃ dadhi bhuñjīta na cāpyaghṛtaśarkaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"><label>ci.24.100</label> nāmudgayūṣaṃ nākṣaudraṃ noṣṇaṃ nāmalakair vinā
  | anyathā janayet kuṣṭhavisarpādīn gadān bahūn | nātmānamudake paśyenna nagnaḥ praviśejjalam
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101"><label>ci.24.101</label>
  dyūtamadyātisevāpratibhutvasākṣitvasamāhvānagoṣṭhīvāditrāṇi na seveta, srajaṃ chatropānakau
  kanakamatītavāsāṃsi na cānyair dhṛtāni dhārayet, brāhmaṇamagniṃ gāṃ ca nocchiṣṭaḥ spṛśet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102"><label>ci.24.102</label> bhavanti cātra yasmin yasminnṛtau ye ye doṣāḥ
  kupyanti dehinām |
  <caesura/>
  teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasāste te vijānatā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103"><label>ci.24.103</label> varṣāsu na pibettoyaṃ pibeccharadi mātrayā |
  <caesura/>
  varṣasu caturo māsān mātrāvadudakaṃ pibet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104"><label>ci.24.104</label> uṣṇaṃ haime vasante ca kāmaṃ śrīṣme tu śītalam
  |
  <caesura/>
  hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau pibennaraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105"><label>ci.24.105</label> śṛtaśītaṃ payo grīṣme prāvṛṭkāle rasaṃ pibet |
  <caesura/>
  yūṣaṃ varṣati, tasyānte prapicchītalaṃ jalam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106"><label>ci.24.106</label> svastha evamato 'nyas tu doṣāhāragatānugaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  snehaṃ saindhavacūrṇena pippalībhiś ca saṃyutam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107"><label>ci.24.107</label> pibedagnivivṛddhyarthaṃ na ca vegān vidhārayet
  |
  <caesura/>
  agnidīptikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ rogāṇāṃ śamanaṃ prati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108"><label>ci.24.108</label> prāvṛṭśaradvasanteṣu samyak snehādimācaret |
  <caesura/>
  kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte vireko bastirīrane || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109"><label>ci.24.109</label> śasyate triṣv api sadā vyāyāmo doṣanāśanaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  bhuktaṃ viruddhamapyannaṃ vyāyāmānna praduṣyati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110"><label>ci.24.110</label> utsargamaithunahāraśodhane syāt tu tanmanāḥ |
  <caesura/>
  neccheddoṣacayāt<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> prājñaḥ pīḍāṃ vā kāyamānasīm
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111"><label>ci.24.111</label> atistrīsaṃprayogāc ca rakṣedātmānamātmavān |
  <caesura/>
  śūlakāsajvaraśvāsakārśyapāṇḍvāmayakṣayāḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112"><label>ci.24.112</label> ativyavājājjāyante rogāś cākṣepakādayaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  āyuṣmanto mandajarā vapurvarṇabalānvitāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113"><label>ci.24.113</label> sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti strīṣu saṃyatāḥ
  |
  <caesura/>
  tribhis tribhir ahobhir vā samīyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114"><label>ci.24.114</label> sarveṣvṛtuṣu, gharmeṣu pakṣāt
  pakṣādvrajedbudhaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  rajasvalāmakāmāṃ ca malināmapriyāṃ tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115"><label>ci.24.115</label> varṇavṛddhāṃ vayovṛddhāṃ tathā
  vyādhiprapīḍitām |
  <caesura/>
  hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitām || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116"><label>ci.24.116</label> sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃ ca tathā pravrajitām api |
  <caesura/>
  sandhyāparvasvagamyāṃ ca nopeyāt pramadāṃ naraḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117"><label>ci.24.117</label> gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā madhyandineṣu ca
  |
  <caesura/>
  lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte 'śuddha eva ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118"><label>ci.24.118</label> kṣudhito vyādhitaś caiva kṣubdhacittaś ca
  mānavaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  vātaviṇmūtravegī ca pipāsaratidurbalaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119"><label>ci.24.119</label> tiryagyonāvayonau ca prāptaśukravidhāraṇam |
  <caesura/>
  duṣṭayonau visargaṃ tu balavānapi varjayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120"><label>ci.24.120</label> retasaś cātimātraṃ tu mūrdhāvaraṇam eva ca |
  <caesura/>
  sthitāvuttānaśayane viśeṣeṇaiva garhitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121"><label>ci.24.121</label> krīḍāyām api medhāvī hitārthī parivarjayet |
  <caesura/>
  rajasvalāṃ prāptavato narasyāniyatātmanaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122"><label>ci.24.122</label> dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hāniradharmaś ca tato bhavet
  |
  <caesura/>
  liṅginīṃ gurupatnīṃ ca sagotrāmatha parvasu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123"><label>ci.24.123</label> vṛddhāṃ ca sandhyayoś cāpi gacchato
  jīvitakṣayaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  garbhiṇyā garbhapīḍā syād vyādhitāyāṃ balakṣayaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124"><label>ci.24.124</label> hīnāṅgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmaṃ
  vandhyāmasaṃvṛte |
  <caesura/>
  deśe 'śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125"><label>ci.24.125</label> kṣudhitaḥ kṣubdhacittaś ca madhyāhne tṛṣito
  'balaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  sthitaś ca hāniṃ śukrasya vāyoḥ kopaṃ ca vindati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126"><label>ci.24.126</label> atiprasaṅgādbhavati śoṣaḥ śukrakṣayāvahaḥ |
  vyādhitasya rujā plīhni mṛtyurmūrcchā ca jāyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127"><label>ci.24.127</label> prayūṣasyardharātre ca vātapitte prakupyataḥ |
  <caesura/>
  tiryagyonāvayanau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128"><label>ci.24.128</label> upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ śukrasya ca kṣayaḥ
  |
  <caesura/>
  uccārite mūtrite ca <ref rend="superscript footnote
  marker">*</ref>retasaś ca vidhāraṇe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129"><label>ci.24.129</label> uttāne ca bhavecchīghraṃ śukrāśmaryās tu
  saṃbhavaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  sarvaṃ pariharettasmād etallokadvaye 'hitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130"><label>ci.24.130</label> śukraṃ copasthitaṃ mohānna sandhāryaṃ
  kathaṃcana |
  <caesura/>
  vayor ūpaguṇopetāṃ tulyaśīlāṃ kulānvitām<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131"><label>ci.24.131</label> abhikāmo 'bhikāmāṃ tu hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭāmalaṅkṛtām |
  <caesura/>
  seveta pramadāṃ yuktyā vājīkaraṇabṛṃhitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132"><label>ci.24.132</label> bhakṣyāḥ saśarkarāḥ kṣīraṃ sasitaṃ rasa eva ca
  |
  <caesura/>
  snānaṃ savyajanaṃ svapno vyavāyānte hitāni tu<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133"><label>ci.24.133</label> mukhamātraṃ samāsena sadvṛttasyaitadīritam |
  <caesura/>
  ārogyamāyurartho vā gāsadbhiḥ prāpyate <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>nṛbhiḥ
  ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne 'nāgatābādhacikitsitaṃ nāma caturviṃśo
  'dhyāyaḥ ||24 ||</p>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28"><label>ci.25.28</label> mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ snigdhā

  vicūrṇya || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29"><label>ci.25.29</label> ekīkṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ pramāya

  māṣān kṛśarāmatho vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36"><label>ci.25.36</label> māsopariṣṭād ghanakuñjitāgrāḥ keśā
  bhavanti bhramarāñjanābhāḥ | keśās tathā 'nye khalatau bhaveyurjarā na cainaṃ
  sahasā 'bhyupaiti || </l>

  <head>ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1"><label>ci.26.1</label> athātaḥ kṣīṇabalīyaṃ vājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"><label>ci.26.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <caesura/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"><label>ci.26.6</label> sevamāno yad aucityād vājīvātyarthavegavān |
  <caesura/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7"><label>ci.26.7</label> bhojanāni vicitrāṇi pānāni vividhāni ca |
  <caesura/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"><label>ci.26.8</label> yāminī sendutilakā kāminī navayauvanā |
  <caesura/>

  <caesura/>

  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10"><label>ci.26.10</label> dveṣyastrīsaṃprayogāc ca klaibyaṃ tanmānasaṃ

  <caesura/>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11"><label>ci.26.11</label> saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaibyaṃ tadaparaṃ

  evam evātibalānāgabalāvidārīśatāvarīṇām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatastvatibalāmudakena,

  pratibedho 'tra <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>pūrvavat;
  prayogamimam upasevamāno varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti strīṣu cākṣayatām, etenaiva
  cūrṇena payo 'vacūrṇya śṛtaśītam abhimathyājyamutpādya madhuyutam upayuñjīta
  sāyaṃprātarekakālaṃ vā, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, evaṃ
  māsam upayujya <ref rend="superscript footnote marker"
  >*</ref>varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12"><label>ci.27.12</label> cakṣuḥkāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā
  bījakasārāgnimanthamūlaṃ niṣkvāthya māṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet, tasmin sidhyati
  citrakamūlānāmakṣamātraṃ kalkaṃ dadyād āmalakarasacaturthabhāgaṃ, tataḥ
  svinnamavatārya sahasrasṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā śītībhūtaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ
  saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta yathābalaṃ, yathāsātmyaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pariharan bhakṣayet |
  jīrṇe mudgāmalakayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtavantam odanam aśnīyāt payasā vā
  māsatrayam; evamābhyāṃ prayogābhyāṃ cakṣuḥ <ref rend="superscript footnote
  marker">*</ref>sauparṇaṃ bhavatyanalpabalaḥ
  strīṣu cākṣayo varṣaśatāyurbhavatīti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"><label>ci.27.13</label> bhavati cātra payasā saha
  siddhāni naraḥ śaṇaphalāni yaḥ | bhakṣayet payasā sārdhaṃ vayastasya na
  śīryate ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne sarvopaghātaśamanīyaṃ
  rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||27 ||</p>
 </div>
 -->

 <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
  <head>aṣṭaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1"><label>ci.28.1</label> athāto <ref rend="superscript
  footnote marker">*</ref>medhāyuṣkāmīyaṃ rasāyanacikitsitaṃ<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"><label>ci.28.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvanatariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3"><label>ci.28.3</label> medhāyuḥkāmaḥ
  śvetāvalgujaphalānyātapapariśuṣkāṇyādāya sūkṣmacūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya snehakumbhe
  saptarātraṃ dhānyarāśau nidadhyāt, saptarātrāduddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ
  prayacched anudite sūrye, uṣṇodakaṃ cānupibet; bhallātakavidhānavaccāgārapraveśaḥ,
  jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe himābhir adbhiḥ pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca payasā
  śarkarāmadhureṇaudanamaśnīyāt; evaṃ ṣaṇmāsānupayujya vigatapāpmā balavarṇopetaḥ śrutanigādī
  smṛtimānarogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | kuṣṭhinaṃ pāṇḍurogiṇamudariṇaṃ vā kṛṣṇāyā
  gormūtreṇāloḍyārdhapalikaṃ piṇḍaṃ vigatalauhitye savitari pāyayet, parāhṇe
  cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam aśnīyāt, evaṃ māsam upayujya smṛtimānarogo
  varṣaśatāyur bhavati | eṣaevopayogaścitrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś ca; citrakamūle viśeṣo dvipalikaṃ
  piṇḍaṃ paraṃ pramāṇaṃ, śeṣaṃ pūrvavat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"><label>ci.28.4</label> hṛtadoṣa eva pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto yathākramamāgāraṃ
  praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalaṃ payasā++āloḍya
  pibet payo 'nupānaṃ vā, tasyāṃ jīrṇāyāṃ yavānnaṃ payasopayuñjīta; tilair vā saha bhakṣayettrīn
  māsān payo 'nupānaṃ, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ; evam upayuñjāno brahmavarcasī
  śrutanigādī bhavati varṣaśatamāyuravāpnoti | trirātropoṣitaś ca trirātramenāṃ bhakṣayet,
  trirātrādūrdhvaṃ payaḥ sarpiriti copayuñjīta | bilvamātraṃ piṇḍaṃ vā payasā++āloḍya pibet,
  evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayujya medhāvī varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"><label>ci.28.5</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
  brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasaṃpātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalampayuñjīta, jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe
  yavāgūmalavaṇaṃ pibet, kṣīrasātmyo vā payasā bhuñjīta, evaṃ saptarātram upayujya brahmavarcasī
  medhāvī bhavati, dvitīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya granthamīpsitamutpādayati naṣṭaṃ cāsya
  prādurbhavati, tṛtīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya dviruccāritaṃ śatamapyavadhārayati, evam
  ekaviṃśatirātram upayujyālakṣmīrapakrāmati; mūrtimatī cainaṃ vāgdevyanupraviśati, sarvāś
  cainaṃ śrutaya upatiṣṭhanti, śrutadharaḥ pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.6"><label>ci.28.6</label> brāhmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprasthaṃ
  viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṃ kuḍavaṃ dve dve pale vacāmṛtayor dvādaśa harītakyāmalakabibhītakāni
  ślakṣṇapiṣṭānyāvāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt, tataḥ pūrvavidhānena mātrāṃ
  yathābalam upayuñjīta, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, pūrvavaccātra parīhāraḥ,
  etenordhvamadhastiryak kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, alakṣmīrapakrāmati, puṣkaravarṇaḥ sthiravayāḥ
  śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyurbhavati; etad eva kuṣṭhaviṣamajvarāpasmāronmādaviṣabhūtagraheṣv
  anyeṣu ca mahāvyādhiṣu saṃśodhanamādiśanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.7"><label>ci.28.7</label> hṛtadoṣa evāgāraṃ praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ
  piṇḍamāmalakamātram abhihutaṃ payasā++āloḍya pibet, jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ityāhāraḥ, evaṃ
  dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta, tato 'sya śrotraṃ vivriyate, dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati,
  trirabhyāsācchrutamādatte, caturdvādaśarātram upayujya sarvaṃ tarati kilbiṣaṃ,
  tārkṣyadarśanamutpadyate, śatāyuś ca bhavati | dve dve pale itarasyā vacāyā viṣkvāthya pibet
  payasā, samānaṃ bhojanaṃ, samāḥ pūrveṇāśiṣaś ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.8"><label>ci.28.8</label> vacāśatapākaṃ vā sarpirdroṇam upayujya
  pañcavarṣaśatāyurbhavati, galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvaramedāṃś cāpahantīti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"><label>ci.28.9</label> ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi āyuṣkāmarasāyanam |
  mantrauṣadhasamāyuktaṃ saṃvatsaraphalapradam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"><label>ci.28.10</label> bilvasya cūrṇaṃ puṣye tu hutaṃ vārān sahasraśaḥ
  | śrīsūktena naraḥ kalye sasuvarṇaṃ dine dine || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"><label>ci.28.11</label> sarpirmdhuyutaṃ lihyādalakṣmīnāśanaṃ param |
  tvacaṃ vihāya bilvasya mūlakvāthaṃ dine dine || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"><label>ci.28.12</label> prāśnīyāt payasā sārdhaṃ snātvā hutvā samāhitaḥ
  | daśasāhassramāyuṣyaṃ smṛtaṃ yuktarathaṃ bhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.13"><label>ci.28.13</label> hutvā bisānāṃ kvāthaṃ tu madhulājaiś ca saṃyutam
  | amoghaṃ śatasāhasraṃ yuktaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.14"><label>ci.28.14</label> suvarṇaṃ padmabījāni madhu lājāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ |
  gavyena payasā pītamalakṣmīṃ pratibedhayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.15"><label>ci.28.15</label> nīlotpaladalakvātho gavyena payasā śṛtaḥ |
  sasuvarṇastilaiḥ sārdhamalakṣmīnāśanaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.16"><label>ci.28.16</label> gavyaṃ payaḥ suvarṇaṃ ca madhūcchiṣṭaṃ ca
  mākṣikam | pītaṃ śatasahasrābhihutaṃ yuktarathaṃ smṛtam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.17"><label>ci.28.17</label> vacāghṛtasuvarṇaṃ ca bilvacūrṇam iti trayam |
  medhyamāyuṣyamārogyapuṣṭisaubhāgyavardhanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.18"><label>ci.28.18</label> vāsāmūlatulākvāthe tailamāvāpya sādhitam | hutvā
  sahasramaśnīyānmedhyamāyuṣyamucyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.19"><label>ci.28.19</label> yāvakāṃstāvakān khādedabhibhūya yavāṃs tathā |
  pippalīmadhusaṃyuktān śikṣā caraṇavadbhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.20"><label>ci.28.20</label> madhvāmalakacūrṇāni suvarṇam iti ca trayam |
  prāśyāriṣṭagṛhīto 'pi mucyate prāṇasaṃśayāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.21"><label>ci.28.21</label> śatāvarīghṛtaṃ samyagupayuktaṃ dine dine |
  sakṣaudraṃ sasuvarṇaṃ ca narendraṃ sthāpayed vaśe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.22"><label>ci.28.22</label> gocandanā mohanikā madhukaṃ mākṣikaṃ madhu |
  suvarṇam iti saṃyogaḥ peyaḥ saubhāgyamicchatā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.23"><label>ci.28.23</label>
  <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>padmanīlotpalakvāthe yaṣṭīmadhukasaṃyute |
  sarpirāsāditaṃ gavyaṃ sasuvarṇaṃ sadā paibet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"><label>ci.28.24</label> payaś cānupibet siddhaṃ teṣām eva samudbhave |
  alakṣmīghnaṃ sadā++āyuṣyaṃ rājyāya subhagāya ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"><label>ci.28.25</label> yatra nodīrito mantro yogeṣveteṣu sādhane |
  śabditā tatra sarvatra gāyatrī tripadā bhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"><label>ci.28.26</label> pāpmānaṃ nāśayantyetā dadyuś cauṣadhayaḥ śriyam
  | kuryurnāgabalaṃ cāpi manuṣyamamaropamam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"><label>ci.28.27</label> satatādhyayanaṃ vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanam |
  tadvidyācāryasevā ca buddhimedhākaro guṇaḥ(gaṇaḥ) || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"><label>ci.28.28</label> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanaṃ jīrṇe vegānāṃ cāvidhāraṇam |
  brahmacaryamahiṃsā ca sāhasānāṃ ca varjanam ||</l>

  'dhyāyaḥ ||28 ||</p>

 <div n="29" type="adhyāya">
  <head>ekonatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1"><label>ci.29.1</label> athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"><label>ci.29.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3"><label>ci.29.3</label> brahmādayo 'sṛjan pūrvamamṛtaṃ somasaṃjñitam |
  <caesura/>
  jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānaṃ tasya vakṣyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4"><label>ci.29.4</label> eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ
  sthānanāmākṛtivīryaviśeṣaiś caturviṃśatidhā bhidyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5"><label>ci.29.5</label> aṃśumān muñjavāṃś caiva candramā rajataprabhaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  dūrvāsomaḥ kanīyāṃś ca śvetākṣaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6"><label>ci.29.6</label> pratānavāṃstālavṛntaḥ karavīro 'ṃśavānapi |
  <caesura/>
  svayaṃprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7"><label>ci.29.7</label> gāyatrastraiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ śākvaras tathā
  |
  <caesura/>
  agniṣṭomo raivataś ca yathokta iti saṃjñitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8"><label>ci.29.8</label> gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaścoḍupatirucyate |
  <caesura/>
  ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nām abhiḥ śubhaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9"><label>ci.29.9</label> sarveṣām eva caiteṣāmeko vidhirupāsane |
  <caesura/>
  sarve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ teṣu vakṣyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10"><label>ci.29.10</label> ato 'nyatamaṃ somam upayuyukṣuḥ
  sarvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ praśaste deśe trivṛtamāgāraṃ kārayitvā hṛtadoṣaḥ
  pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu aṃśumantamādāyādhvarakalpenāhṛtam
  abhiṣutam abhihutaṃ cāntarāgāre kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaḥ somakandaṃ suvarṇasūcyā vidārya payo
  gṛhṇīyāt sauvarṇe (<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>rājate vā) pātre
  'ñjalimātraṃ, tataḥ sakṛdevopayuñjīta nāsvādayan, tata upaspṛśya śeṣamapsvavasādya
  yamaniyamābhyām ātmānaṃ saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantarataḥ suhṛdbhir upāsyamāno viharet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11"><label>ci.29.11</label> rasāyanaṃ pītavāṃs tu nivāte tanmanāḥ śuciḥ |
  <caesura/>
  āsīta tiṣṭhet krāmec ca na kathaṃcana saṃviśet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12"><label>ci.29.12</label> sāyaṃ vā bhuktavānupaśrutaśāntiḥ kuśaśayyāyāṃ
  kṛṣṇājinottarāyāṃ suhṛdbhir upāsyamānaḥ śayīta, tṛṣito vā śītodakamātrāṃ pibet (<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>aśanāyito vā kṣīraṃ); tataḥ
  prātarutthāyopaśrutaśāntiḥ kṛtamaṅgalo gāṃ spṛṣṭvā tatahaivāsīta, tasya jīrṇe some
  chardirutpadyate, tataḥ śoṇitāktaṃ kṛmivyāmiśraṃ charditavate sāyaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ kṣīraṃ vitaret;
  tatastṛtīye 'hani kṛmivyāmiśramatisāryate, sa tenāniṣṭapratigrahabhuktaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair
  vinirmuktaḥ śuddhatanurbhavati, tataḥ sāyaṃ snātāya pūrvavadeva kṣīraṃ vitaret,
  kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ cainaṃ śayyāyāṃ śāyayet; tataś caturthe 'hani tasya śvayathurutpadyate,
  tataḥ sarvāṅgebhyaḥ kṛmayo niṣkrāmanti, tadahaś ca <ref rend="superscript footnote
     marker">*</ref>śayyāyāṃ pāṃśubhir avakīryamāṇaḥ śayīta, tataḥ sāyaṃ
  pūrvavadeva kṣīraṃ vitaret; evaṃ pañcamaṣaṣṭhayor divasayor varteta, kevalamubhayakālamasmai
  kṣīraṃ vitaret; tataḥ saptame 'hani nirmāṃsastvagasthibhūtaḥ kevalaṃ
  somaparigrahādevocchvasiti, tadahaś ca kṣīreṇa sukhoṣṇena pariṣicya
  tilamadhukacandanānuliptadehaṃ payaḥ pāyayet; tato 'ṣṭame 'hani prātareva kṣīrapariṣiktaṃ
  candanapradigdhāgātraṃ payaḥ pāyayitvā pāṃśuśayyāṃ samutsṛjya kṣaumavastrāstṛtāyāṃ śayyāyāṃ
  śāyayet, tato 'sya māṃsamāpyāyyate, tvak cāvadalati, dantanakharomāṇi cāsya patanti; tasya
  navamadivasāt prabhṛtyaṇutailābhyaṅgaḥ somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ; tato daśame 'hanyetadeva
  vitaret, tato 'sya tvak sthiratām upaiti; evam ekādaśadvādaśayor varteta; tatastrayodaśāt
  prabhṛti somavalkakaṣāyapariṣekaḥ, evamāṣoḍaśādvarteta; tataḥ saptadaśāṣṭādaśayor divasayor 
  daśanā jāyante śikhariṇaḥ snigdhavajravaidūryasphaṭikaprakāśāḥ samāḥ sthirāḥ sahiṣṇavaḥ, tadā
  prabhṛti cānavaiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ kṣīrayavāgūm upaseveta yāvat pañcaviṃśatiriti; tato 'smai
  dadyācchālyodanaṃ mṛdūbhayakālaṃ payasā, tato 'sya nakhā jāyante
  vidrumendragopakataruṇādityaprakāśāḥ, sthirāḥ snigdhā lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ keśāś ca sūkṣmā
  jāyante, tvak ca nīlotpalātasīpuṣpavaidūryaprakāśā; ūrdhvaṃ ca māsāt keśān vāpayet, vāpayitvā
  cośīracandanakṛṣṇatilakalkaiḥ śiraḥ pradihyāt payasā vā snāpayet; tato 'syānantaraṃ
  saptarātrāt keśā jāyante bhramarāñjananibhāḥ kuñcitāḥ sthirāḥ snigdhāḥ; tatas trirātrāt<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> prathamāvasathaparisarānniṣkramya muhūrtaṃ sthitvā
  punarevāntaḥ praviśet, tato 'sya balātailamabhyaṅgārthe 'vacāryaṃ, yavapiṣṭamudvartanārthe,
  sukhoṣṇaṃ ca payaḥ pariṣekārthe, ajakarṇakaṣāyamutsādanārthe, sośīraṃ kūpodakaṃ snānārthe,
  candanamanulepārthe, āmalakarasavimiśrāś cāsya yūṣasūpavikalpāḥ, kṣīramadhukasiddhaṃ ca
  kṛṣṇatilamavacāraṇārthe, evaṃ daśarātraṃ; tato 'nyaddaśarātraṃ dvitīye parisare varteta;
  tatastṛtīye parisare sthirīkurvannātmānamanyaddaśarātramāsīta, kiñcidātapapavanān vā seveta,
  punaś cāntaḥ praviśet, na cātmānamādarśe 'psu vā nirīkṣeta rūpaśālitvāt ; tato 'nyaddaśarātraṃ
  krodhādīn <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>pariharet, evaṃ sarveṣām
  upayogavikalpaḥ | viśeṣatas tu vallīpratānakṣupakādayaḥ somā brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyair
  bhakṣayitavyāḥ | teṣāṃ tu pramāṇamardhacatuṣkamuṣṭayaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13"><label>ci.29.13</label> aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇe pātre 'bhiṣuṇuyāt,
  candramasaṃ rājate; tāvupayujyāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryamavāpyeśānaṃ devamanupraviśati, śeṣāṃstu
  tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā rohite vā carmaṇi vitate; śūdravarjaṃ tribhir varṇaiḥ somā upayoktavyāḥ |
  tataś caturthe māse paurṇamāsyāṃ śucau deśe brāhmaṇānarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalo niṣkramya yathoktaṃ
  vrajediti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14"><label>ci.29.14</label> oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujya vicakṣaṇaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navāṃ dhārayate tanum || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15"><label>ci.29.15</label> nāgnir na toyaṃ na viṣaṃ na śastraṃ nāstram eva
  ca |
  <caesura/>
  tasyālamāyuḥkṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16"><label>ci.29.16</label> bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ prasrutānāmanekadhā |
  <caesura/>
  kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17"><label>ci.29.17</label> kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanamuttarāṃś ca kurūn api |
  <caesura/>
  yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vā tatrāpratihatā gatiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18"><label>ci.29.18</label> kandarpa iva rūpeṇa kāntyā candra ivāparaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19"><label>ci.29.19</label> sāṅgopāṅgāṃś ca nikhilān vedān vindati tattvataḥ
  |
  <caesura/>
  caraty amoghasaṅkalpo devavac cākhilaṃ jagat || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20"><label>ci.29.20</label> sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa pañca ca |
  <caesura/>
  tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante nipatanti ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21"><label>ci.29.21</label> ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ somasyāharahas tadā |
  <caesura/>
  śuklasya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu bhavet pañcadaśacchadaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.22"><label>ci.29.22</label> śīryate patramekaikaṃ divase divase punaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  kṛṣṇapakṣakṣaye cāpi latā bhavati kevalā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.23"><label>ci.29.23</label> aṃśumān ājyagandhas tu kandavān rajataprabhaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  kadalyākārakandas tu muñjavāṃ llaśunacchadaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.24"><label>ci.29.24</label> candramāḥ kanakābhāso jale carati sarvadā |
  <caesura/>
  garuḍāhṛtanāmā ca śvetākṣaś cāpi pāṇḍurau || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.25"><label>ci.29.25</label> sarpanirmokasadṛśau tau vṛkṣāgrāvalambinau |
  <caesura/>
  <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>tathā 'nye maṇḍalaiś citraiś citritā iva bhānti
  te || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.26"><label>ci.29.26</label> sarva eva tu vijñeyāḥ somāḥ pañcadaśacchadāḥ |
  <caesura/>
  kṣīrakandalatāvantaḥ patrair nānāvidhaiḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.27"><label>ci.29.27</label> himavaty arbude sahye mahendre malaye tathā |
  <caesura/>
  śrīparvate devagirau girau devasahe tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28"><label>ci.29.28</label> pāriyātre ca vindhye ca devasunde hrade tathā |
  <caesura/>
  uttareṇa vitastāyāḥ pravṛddhā ye mahīdharāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.29"><label>ci.29.29</label> haṣṭhavat plavate tatra candramāḥ somasattamaḥ |
  <caesura/>
  tasyoddeśeṣu cāpyanti muñjavān aṃśumān api || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.30"><label>ci.29.30</label> tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy asti muñjavānaṃśumānapi |
  <caesura/>
  kāśmīreṣu saro divyaṃ nāmnā kṣudrakamānasam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.31"><label>ci.29.31</label> gāyatras traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṅkto jāgataḥ <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>śākvaras tathā | atra santy apare cāpi somāḥ
  somasamaprabhāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.29.32"><label>ci.29.32</label> yaiś cātra mandabhāgyais te bhiṣajaś cāpamānitāḥ
  |
  <caesura/>
  na tān paśyanty adharmiṣṭhāḥ kṛtaghnāś cāpi mānavāḥ |
  <caesura/>
  bheṣajadveṣiṇaś cāpi brāhmaṇadveṣiṇas tathā ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ
  rasāyanacikitsitaṃ nāmaikonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||29 ||</p>
 </div>
