  <head>ekonacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.1"><label>ci.39.1</label> athāta āturopadravacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.2"><label>ci.39.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.3"><label>ci.39.3</label> snehapītasya vāntasya viriktasya srutāsṛjaḥ |
  nirūḍhasya ca kāyāgnir mando bhavati dehinaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.4"><label>ci.39.4</label> so 'gnair atyarthagurubhir upayuktaiḥ praśāmyati |
  alpo mahadbhir bahubhiś chādito 'gnir ivendhanaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.5"><label>ci.39.5</label> sa cālpair laghubhiś cānnair upayuktair vivardhate
  | kāṣṭhair aṇubhir alpaiś ca sandhukṣita ivānalaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.6"><label>ci.39.6</label> hṛtadoṣapramāṇena sadāhāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ | trīṇi
  cātra pramāṇāni prastho 'rdhāḍhakam āḍhakam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.7"><label>ci.39.7</label> tatrāvaraṃ prasthamātraṃ dve śeṣe madhyamottame |
  prasthe parisrute deyā yavāgūḥ khalpataṇḍulā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.8"><label>ci.39.8</label> dve caivārdhāḍhake deye tisraś cāpy āḍhake gate |
  vilepīmucitādbhaktāc caturthāṃśakṛtāṃ tataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.9"><label>ci.39.9</label> dadyād uktena vidhinā klinnasikthāmapicchilām |
  <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>agnigdhalavaṇaṃ svacchamudgayūṣayutaṃ tataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.10a"><label>ci.39.10a</label> aṃśadvayapramāṇena dadyāt susvinnam odanam | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.10b"><label>ci.39.10b</label>tatas tu kṛtasaṃjñena hṛdyenendriyabodhinā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.11"><label>ci.39.11</label> trīn aṃśān vitared bhoktum āturāyaudanaṃ mṛdu |
  tato yathocitaṃ bhaktaṃ bhoktum asmai vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.12"><label>ci.39.12</label> lāvaiṇahariṇādīnāṃ rasair dadyāt susaṃskṛtaiḥ |
  hīnamadhyottameṣv eṣu virekeṣu prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.13a"><label>ci.39.13a</label> ekadvitriguṇaḥ samyag āhārasya kramas tv ayam
  |</l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.13b"><label>ci.39.13b</label>kaphapittādhikān madyanityān hīnaviśodhitān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.14a"><label>ci.39.14a</label> peyā 'bhiṣyandayetteṣāṃ tarpaṇādikramo hitaḥ | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.14b"><label>ci.39.14b</label>vedanālābhaniyamaśokavaicittyahetubhiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.15"><label>ci.39.15</label> narān upoṣitāṃś cāpi viriktavad upācaret |
  āḍhakārdhāḍhakaprasthasaṃkhyā hy eṣā virecane || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.16"><label>ci.39.16</label> śleṣmāntatvād virekasya na tām icchati tadvidaḥ
  | eko virekaḥ śleṣmānto na dvitīyo 'sti kaś cana || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.17"><label>ci.39.17</label> balaṃ yat trividhaṃ proktam atas tatra kramas
  tridhā | tatrānukramamekaṃ tu balasthaḥ sakṛdācaret || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.18"><label>ci.39.18</label> dvirācarenmadhyabalastrīn vārān durbalas tathā |
  kecid evaṃ kramaṃ prāhur mandamadhyottamāgniṣu || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.19"><label>ci.39.19</label> saṃsargeṇa vivṛddhe 'gnau doṣakopabhayādbhajet |
  prāk svādutiktau snigdhāmlalavaṇān kaṭukaṃ tataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.20"><label>ci.39.20</label> svādvamlalavaṇān bhūyaḥ svādutiktāvataḥ param |
  snigdharūkṣān rasāṃś caiva vyatyāsāt svasthavattataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.21"><label>ci.39.21</label> kevalaṃ snehapīto vā vānto yaś cāpi kevalam | sa
  saptarātraṃ manujo bhuñjīta laghu bhojanam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.22"><label>ci.39.22</label> kṛtaḥ sirāvyadho yasya kṛtaṃ yasya ca śodhanam |
  sa nā pariharenmāsaṃ yāvadvā balavān bhavet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.23"><label>ci.39.23</label> tryahaṃ tryahaṃ parihared ekaikaṃ bastim
  āturaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> || tṛtīye tu parīhāre yathāyogaṃ
  samācaret || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.24"><label>ci.39.24</label> tailapūrṇāmṛdbhāṇḍasadharmāṇo vraṇāturāḥ |
  snigdhaśuddhākṣirogārtā jvarātīsāriṇaś ca ye || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.25"><label>ci.39.25</label> krudhyataḥ kupitaṃ pittaṃ kuryāt tāṃs tān
  upadravān | āyāsyataḥ śocato vā cittaṃ vibhramam ṛcchati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.26"><label>ci.39.26</label> maithunopagamād ghorān vyādhīn āpnoti durmatiḥ |
  ākṣepakaṃ pakṣaghātam aṅgapragraham eva ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.27"><label>ci.39.27</label> guhyapradeśe śvayathuṃ kāsaśvāsau ca dāruṇau |
  rudhiraṃ śukravac cāpi sarajaskaṃ pravartate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.28"><label>ci.39.28</label> labhate ca divāsvapnāttāṃstān vyādhīn
  kaphātmakān | plīhodaraṃ pratiśyāyaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ śvayathuṃ jvaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.29"><label>ci.39.29</label> mohaṃ sadanam aṅgānām avipākaṃ tathā 'rucim |
  tamasā cābhibhūtas tu svapnam evābhinandati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.30"><label>ci.39.30</label> uccaiḥ saṃbhāṣaṇād vāyuḥ śirasy āpādayed rujam |
  <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>āndhyaṃ jāḍyamajighratvaṃ bādhiryaṃ mūkatāṃ
  tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31a"><label>ci.39.31a</label> hanumokṣamadhīmanthamarditaṃ ca sudāruṇam | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31b"><label>ci.39.31b</label> netrastambhaṃ nimeṣaṃ vā tṛṣṇāṃ kāsaṃ
  prajāgaram || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.32"><label>ci.39.32</label> labhate dantacālaṃ ca tāṃs tāṃś cānyān upadravān
  | yānayānena labhate chardimūrcchābhramaklamān || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.33"><label>ci.39.33</label> tathaivāṅgagrahaṃ ghoram indriyāṇāṃ ca vibhramam
  | cirāsanāttathā sthānāc chroṇyāṃ bhavati vedanā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.34"><label>ci.39.34</label> aticaṅkramaṇād vāyur jaṅghayoḥ kurute rujaḥ |
  sakthipraśoṣaṃ śophaṃ vā pādaharṣam athāpi vā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35a"><label>ci.39.35a</label> śītasaṃbhogatoyānāṃ sevā mārutavṛddhaye | </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35b"><label>ci.39.35b</label>tato 'ṅgamardaviṣṭambhaśūlādhmānapravepakāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.36"><label>ci.39.36</label> vātātapābhyāṃ vaivarṇyaṃ jvaraṃ cāpi samāpnuyāt
  | viruddhādhyaśanān mṛtyuṃ vyādhiṃ vā ghoram ṛcchati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.37"><label>ci.39.37</label> asātmyabhojanaṃ hanyād balavarṇam asaṃśayam |
  anātmavantaḥ paśuvad bhuñjate ye 'pramāṇataḥ | rogānīkasya te mūlam ajīrṇaṃ prāpnuvanti hi || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.38"><label>ci.39.38</label> vyāpadāṃ kāraṇaṃ vīkṣya vyāpatsv etāsu buddhimān
  | prayatetāturārogye pratyanīkena hetunā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.39.39"><label>ci.39.39</label> viriktavāntair hariṇaiṇalāvakāḥ śaśaś ca sevyaḥ
  samayūratittiriḥ | saṣaṣṭikāś caiva purāṇaśālayas tathaiva mudgā laghu yac ca kīrtitam ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne āturopadravacikitsitaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo
  'dhyāyaḥ ||39 ||</p>
 </div>




 <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
  <head>catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1"><label>ci.40.1</label> athāto dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ
  vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"><label>ci.40.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3"><label>ci.40.3</label> dhūmaḥ pañcavidho bhavati tadyathā prāyogikaḥ,
  snaihiko, vair enikaḥ, kāsaghno, vāmanīyaś ceti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4"><label>ci.40.4</label> tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena ślakṣṇapiṣṭena
  dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍamaṅgulipariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ veṣṭayitvā lepayed eṣā vartiḥ <ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>prāyogike,
  snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiḥ snehamiśraiḥ snaihike,
  śirovirecanadravyair vair ecane,
  bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukāsamardahiṅgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭaśṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
  kāsaharaiś ca kāsaghne, snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭakāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakṛmiprabhṛtibhir
  vāmanīyaiś ca vāmanīye || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5"><label>ci.40.5</label> tatra bastinetradravyair dhūmanetradravyāṇi
  vyākhyātāni bhavanti | dhūmanetraṃ tu kaniṣṭhikāpariṇāhamagre kalāyamātrasroto mūle
  'ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ dhūmavartipraveśasroto 'ṅgulānyaṣṭacatvāriṃśat prāyogike, dvātriṃśat
  snehane, caturviṃśatirvair ecane, ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ kāsaghne vāmanīye ca | ete 'pi
  kolāsthimātracchidre bhavataḥ | vraṇanetramaṣṭāṅgulaṃ vraṇadhūpanārthaṃ kalāyaparimaṇḍalaṃ
  kulatthavāhisrota iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6"><label>ci.40.6</label> atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā ṛjvadhodṛṣṭiratandritaḥ
  <ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>snehāktadīpatāgrāṃ vartiṃ netrasrotasi
  praṇidhāya dhūmaṃ pibet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7"><label>ci.40.7</label> mukhena taṃ pibet pūrvaṃ nāsikābhyāṃ tataḥ pibet |
  mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītaṃ ca nāsayā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8"><label>ci.40.8</label> mukhena dhūmamādāya nāsikābhyāṃ na nirharet | tena
  hi pratilomena dṛṣṭis tatra nihanyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9"><label>ci.40.9</label> viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ ghrāṇenādadīta, snaihikaṃ
  mukhanāsābhyāṃ, nāsikayā vair ecanikaṃ, mukhenaivetarau || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"><label>ci.40.10</label> tatra prāyogike vartiṃ vyapagataśarakāṇḍāṃ
  nivātātapaśuṣkāmaṅgāreṣv avadīpya netramūlasrotasi prayujyadhūmamāhareti brūyāt; evaṃ snehanaṃ
  vair ecanikaṃ ca kuryād iti | itarayor vyapetadhūmāṅgāre<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> sthire samāhite śarāve prakṣipya vartiṃ
  mūlacchidreṇānyena śarāveṇa pidhāya tasmin chidre netramūlaṃ saṃyojya dhūmamāseveta, praśānte
  dhūme vartimavaśiṣṭāṃ prakṣipya punarapi dhūmaṃ pāyayed ādoṣaviśuddheḥ; eṣa dhūmapānopāyavidhiḥ
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11"><label>ci.40.11</label> tatra
  śokaśramabhayāmarṣauṣṇyaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchādāhapipāsāpāṇḍurogatāluśoṣacchardiśiro
  'bhighātodgārāpatarpitatimirapramehodarādhmānordhvavātārtā
  bālavṛddhadurbalaviriktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣīṇakṣatoraskamadhughṛtad
  adhidugdhamatsyamadyayavāgūpītālpakaphāś ca na dhūmamāseveran || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12"><label>ci.40.12</label> akālapītaḥ kurute bhramaṃ mūrcchāṃ śirorujam |
  ghrāṇaśrotrākṣijihvānām upaghātaṃ ca dāruṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13"><label>ci.40.13</label> ādyās tu trayo dhūmā dvādaśasu kāleṣūpādeyāḥ |
  tadyathā
  kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanadivāsvapnamaithunacchardimūtroccārahasitaruṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv
  iti | tatra vibhāgo mūtroccārakṣavathuhasitaruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ,
  snānacchardivāsvapnānteṣu vair ecanikaḥ, dantaprakṣālanasya snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu
  prāyogika iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14"><label>ci.40.14</label> tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati, snehād upalepāc
  ca; vair ecanaḥ śleṣmāṇamutkleśyāpakarṣati, raukṣyāttaikṣṇyādauṣṇyādvaiśadyācca; prāyogikaḥ
  śleṣmāṇamutkleśayatyutkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣati śamayati vātaṃ sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15"><label>ci.40.15</label> bhavati cātra naro dhūmopayogācca
  prasannendriyavāṅmanāḥ | dṛḍhakeśadvijaśmaśruḥ sugandhiviśadānanaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16"><label>ci.40.16</label> tathā
  kāsaśvāsārocakāsyopalepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrathatandrānidrāhanumanyāstambhāḥ
  pīnasaśirorogakarṇākṣiśūlā vātakaphanimittāś cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17"><label>ci.40.17</label> tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyāḥ | tatra yogo
  rogapraśamanaḥ, ayogo rogāpraśamanaḥ,
  tālugalaśoṣaparidāhapipāsāmūrcchābhramamadakarṇakṣveḍadṛṣṭināsārogadaurbalyānyatiyogo<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> janayati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18"><label>ci.40.18</label> prāyogikaṃ trīṃstrīnucchvāsānādadīta
  mukhanāsikābhyāṃ ca paryāyāṃstrīṃś caturo veti, snaihikaṃ yāvadaśrupravṛttiḥ, vair
  ecanikamādoṣadarśanāt, tilataṇḍulayavāgūpītena pātavyo vāmanīyaḥ, grāsāntareṣu kāsaghna iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19"><label>ci.40.19</label> vraṇadhūmaṃ śarāvasaṃpuṭopanītena netreṇa
  vraṇamānayet, dhūmapānādvedanopaśamo vraṇavaiśadyamāsrāvopaśamaś ca bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20"><label>ci.40.20</label> vidhireṣa samāsena dhūmasyābhihito mayā |
  nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ niravaśeṣataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21"><label>ci.40.21</label> auṣadhamauṣadhasiddho vā sneho nāsikābhyāṃ
  dīyata iti nasyam | taddvividhaṃ śirovirecanaṃ, snehanaṃ ca | taddvividham api pañcadhā |
  tadyathā nasyaṃ, śirovirecanaṃ, pratimarśo, avapīḍaḥ, pradhamanaṃ ca | teṣu nasyaṃ pradhānaṃ
  śirovirecanaṃ ca; nasyavikalpaḥ pratimarśaḥ, śirovirecanavikalpo 'vapīḍaḥ pradhamanaṃ ca; tato
  nasyaśabdaḥ pañcadhā niyamitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22"><label>ci.40.22</label> tatra yaḥ snehanārthaṃ śūnyaśirasāṃ
  grīvāskandhorasāṃ ca balajananārthaṃ dṛṣṭiprasādajananārthaṃ vā sneho vidhīyate tasmin
  vaiśeṣiko nasyaśabdaḥ | tat tu deyaṃ vātābhibhūte śirasi
  dantakeśaśmaśruprapātadāruṇakarṇaśūlakarṇakṣveḍatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogāsyaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprādurbhāvadāruṇaprabodheṣu
  vātapaittikeṣu mukharogeṣv anyeṣu ca vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23"><label>ci.40.23</label> śirovirecanaṃ śleṣmaṇā
  'bhivyāptatālukaṇṭhaśirasāmarocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasārdhāvabhedakakṛmipratiśyāyāpasmāragandhājñāneṣv
  anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu kaphajeṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyais tatsiddhena vā sneheneti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24"><label>ci.40.24</label> tatraitaddvividhamapyabhuktavato 'nnakāle
  pūrvāhṇe śleṣmarogiṇāṃ, madhyāhne pittarogiṇāṃ, aparāhṇe vātarogiṇām || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25"><label>ci.40.25</label> atha puruṣāya śirovirecanīyāya
  tyaktamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle dantakāṣṭhadhūmapānābhyāṃ viśuddhavaktrasrotase
  pāṇitāpaparisvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne veśmanyuttānaśāyine
  prasāritakaracaraṇāya kiñcit pravilambitaśirase vastrācchāditanetrāya
  vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotasi dakṣiṇahastena sneham uṣṇāmbunā
  prataptaṃ rajatasuvarṇatāmramaṇimṛtpātraśuktīnām anyatamasthaṃ śuktyā<ref
  rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> picunā vā sukhoṣṇaṃ snehamadrutam āsiñced
  avyavacchinnadhāraṃ yathā netre na prāpnoti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26"><label>ci.40.26</label> snehe 'vasicyamāne tu śiro naiva prakampayet |
  na kupyen na prabhāṣec ca na kṣuyān na haset tathā || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27"><label>ci.40.27</label> etair hi vihataḥ sneho na samyak pratipadyate |
  tataḥ kāsapratiśyāyaśiro 'kṣigadasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28"><label>ci.40.28</label> tasya pramāṇamaṣtau bindavaḥ
  pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsṛtāḥ prathamā mātrā, dvitīyā śuktiḥ, tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktiḥ, ityetāstisro
  mātrā yathābalaṃ prayojyāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"><label>ci.40.29</label> snehanasyaṃ nopagilet kathaṃ cid api buddhimān
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30"><label>ci.40.30</label> śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti vadanād yathā |
  kaphotkleśabhayāccainaṃ niṣṭhīvedavidhārayan || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31"><label>ci.40.31</label> datte ca punarapi saṃsvedya galakapolādīn
  dhūmamāseveta, bhojayeccainam abhiṣyandi, tato 'syācārikam ādiśet;
  rajodhūmasnehātapamadyadravapānaśiraḥsnānātiyānakrodhādīni ca pariharet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32"><label>ci.40.32</label> tasya yogātiyogāyogānāmidaṃ vijñānaṃ bhavati || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33"><label>ci.40.33</label> lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge sukhasvapnaprabodhanam |
  vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhirindiryāṇāṃ manaḥsukham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34"><label>ci.40.34</label> kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ |
  lakṣaṇaṃ mūrdhnayatisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ tatrāvacārayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"><label>ci.40.35</label> ayoge vātavaiguṇyamindriyāṇāṃ ca rūkṣatā |
  rogāśāntiś ca tatreṣṭaṃ bhūyo nasyaṃ prayojayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36"><label>ci.40.36</label> catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā tathā 'ṣṭau vā
  yathābalam | śirovirekasnehasya pramāṇam abhinirdiśet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37"><label>ci.40.37</label> nasye trīṇyupadiṣṭāni lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ |
  śuddha(śuddhi)hīnātisaṃjñāni viśeṣācchāstracintakaiḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38"><label>ci.40.38</label> lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ suddhiḥ srotasāṃ vyādhinirjayaḥ
  | cittendriyaprasādaś ca śirasaḥ śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39"><label>ci.40.39</label> kaṇḍūpadehau gurutā srotasāṃ kaphasaṃsravaḥ |
  mūrdhni hīnaviśuddhe tu lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40"><label>ci.40.40</label> mastuluṅgāgamo vātavṛddhirindriyavibhramaḥ |
  śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41"><label>ci.40.41</label> hīnātiśuddhe śirasi kaphavātaghnamācaret |
  samyagviśuddhe śirasi sarpirnasyaṃ niṣecayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42"><label>ci.40.42</label> (ekāntaraṃ dvyanataraṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā punaḥ
  punaḥ | ekaviṃśatirātraṃ vā yāvadvā sādhu manyate ||) </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"><label>ci.40.43</label> mārutenābhibhūtasya vā 'tyantaṃ yasya dehinaḥ |
  dvikālaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ nasyaṃ tasya vijānatā<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref>
  ||) </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44"><label>ci.40.44</label> avapīḍastu
  śirovirecanavadabhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭavisaṃjñebhyo dadyāc chirocirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam
  avapiṣyāvapīḍya<ref rend="superscript footnote marker">*</ref> ca,</l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a"><label>ci.40.44a</label> śarkarekṣurasakṣīraghṛtamāṃsarasānām anyatamaṃ
  kṣīṇānāṃ śoṇitapitte ca vidadhyāt || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"><label>ci.40.45</label> kṛśadurbalabhīrūṇāṃ sukumārasya yoṣitām | śṛtāḥ
  snehāḥ śiraḥśuddhyai kalkastebhyo<ref rend="superscript
  footnote marker">*</ref> yathā hitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46"><label>ci.40.46</label> cetovikārakṛmiviṣābhipannānāṃ cūrṇaṃ pradhamet
  || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47"><label>ci.40.47</label> nasyena parihartavyo bhutavānapatarpito
  'tyarthataruṇapratiśyāyī garbhiṇī pītasnehodakamadyadravo 'jīrṇī dattabastiḥ kruddho
  garārtastṛṣitaḥ śokābhibhūtaḥ ānto bālo vṛddho vegāvarodhitaḥ<ref rend="superscript footnote
  marker">*</ref> śiraḥsnātukāmaś ceti; anārtave cābhre nasyadhūmau pariharet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"><label>ci.40.48</label> tatra
  hīnātimātrātiśītoṣṇasahasāpradānādatipravilambitaśirasa ucchiṅghato vicalato 'bhyavaharato vā
  pratiṣiddhapradānāc ca vyāpado bhavanti tṛṣṇodgārādayo doṣanimittāḥ kṣayajāś ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49"><label>ci.40.49</label> bhavataś cātra nasye śirovireke ca vyāpado
  dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ | doṣotkleśāt kṣayāccaiva vijñeyāstā yathākramam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50"><label>ci.40.50</label> doṣokleśanimittās tu jayecchamanaśodhanaiḥ | atha
  kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51"><label>ci.40.51</label> pratimarśaś caturdaśasu kāleṣūpādeyaḥ; tadyathā
  talpotthitena, prakṣālitadantena, gṛhānnirgacchatā, vyāyāmavyavāyādhvapariśrāntena,
  mūtroccārakavalāñjanānte, bhuktavatā, charditavatā, divāsvapnotthitena, sāyaṃ ceti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52"><label>ci.40.52</label> tatra talpotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo
  rātrāvupacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ malam upahanti manaḥprasādaṃ ca karoti, prakṣālitadantenāsevito
  dantānāṃ dṛḍhatāṃ vadanasaugandhyaṃ cāpādayati, gṛhānnirgacchatā sevito nāsāseotasaḥ
  klinnatayā rajodhūmo vā na bādhate, vyāyāmamaithunādhvapariśrāntenāsevitaḥ śramam upahanti,
  mūtroccārānte sevito dṛṣṭergurutvam apanayati, kavalāñjanānte sevito dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati,
  bhuktavatā sevitaḥ srotasāṃ viśuddhiṃ laghutāṃ cāpādayati, vāntenāsevitaḥ srotovilagnaṃ
  śleṣmāṇamapohya bhaktākāṅkṣāmāpādayati, divāsvapnotthitenāsevito nidrāśeṣaṃ gurutvaṃ malaṃ
  cāpohya cittaikāgryaṃ janayati, sāyaṃ cāsevitaḥ sukhanidrāprabodhaṃ ceti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53"><label>ci.40.53</label> īṣaducchiṅghataḥ sneho yāvadvaktraṃ prapadyate |
  nasye niṣiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54"><label>ci.40.54</label> nasyena rogāḥ śāmyanti narāṇāmūrdhvajatrujāḥ |
  indriyāṇāṃ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyaṃ sugandhi ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55"><label>ci.40.55</label> hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ balam |
  valīpalitakhālityavyaṅgānāṃ cāpyasaṃbhavam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56"><label>ci.40.56</label> tailaṃ kaphe savāte syāt kevale pavane vasām |
  dadyātsarpiḥ sadā pitte majjānaṃ ca samārute || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57"><label>ci.40.57</label> caturvidhasya snehasya vidhirevaṃ prakīrtitaḥ |
  śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailaṃ vidhīyate || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58"><label>ci.40.58</label> ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kavalagrahaṇe vidhim |
  caturdhā kavalaḥ snehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59"><label>ci.40.59</label> sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte svāduśītaiḥ
  prasādanaḥ | pitte kaṭvamlalavaṇai rūkṣoṣṇaiḥ śodhanaḥ kaphe || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60"><label>ci.40.60</label> kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇai ropaṇo vraṇe |
  caturvidhasya caivāsya viśeṣo 'yaṃ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61"><label>ci.40.61</label> tatra trikaṭukavacāsarṣapaharītakīkalkamāloḍya
  tailaśuktasurāmūtrakṣāramadhūnāmanyatamena salavaṇam abhiprataptam
  upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśo dhārayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62"><label>ci.40.62</label> sukhaṃ saṃcāryate yā tu mātrā sa (sā) kavalaḥ
  smṛtaḥ | asaṃcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63"><label>ci.40.63</label> tāvac ca dhārayitavyo 'nanyamanasonnatadehena
  yāvaddoṣaparipūrṇakapolatvaṃ nāsāsrotonayanapariplāvaś ca bhavati tadā vimoktavyaḥ, punaś
  cānyo grahītavya iti || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64"><label>ci.40.64</label> evaṃ snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmlasaṃbhṛtāḥ |
  kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāṃ ca kavalā doṣato hitāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65"><label>ci.40.65</label> vyādher apacayastuṣṭirvaiśadyaṃ vaktralāghavam |
  indiryāṇāṃ prasādaś ca kavale śuddhilakṣaṇam || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66"><label>ci.40.66</label> hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśāvarasajñānam eva ca |
  atiyogān mukhe pākaḥ śoṣatṛṣṇāruciklamāḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67"><label>ci.40.67</label> śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavanty eva na saṃśayaḥ |
  tilā nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68"><label>ci.40.68</label> sakṣaudro dagdhavaktrasya gaṇḍūṣo dāhanāśanaḥ |
  kavalasya vidhirhyeṣa samāsena prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69"><label>ci.40.69</label> vibhajya bheṣajaṃ buddhyā kurvīta pratisāraṇam |
  kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇaṃ ceti caturvidham || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70"><label>ci.40.70</label> aṅgulyagrapraṇītaṃ tu yathāsvaṃ mukharogiṇām |
  tasmin yogamayogaṃ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet || </l>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71"><label>ci.40.71</label> tān eva śamayed vyādhīn kavalo yān apohati |
  doṣaghnam anabhiṣyandi bhojayec ca tathā naram ||</l>

  <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthāne dhūmanasyakavalagrahacikitsitaṃ nāma
  catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.72"/>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.73"/>
  <l xml:id="SS.4.40.74"/>













 </div>

 <div>
  <p ana="trailer">iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā suśrutena
  viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ cikitsāsthānaṃ samāptam || </p>















 </div>


 </div>
